Options	O	O

PASTA	O	B-Application
estimates	O	O
alignments	O	O
and	O	O
maximum	O	O
likelihood	O	O
(	O	O
ML	O	O
)	O	O
trees	O	B-Data_Structure
from	O	O
unaligned	O	O
sequences	O	O

an	O	O

approach	O	O
.	O	O

In	O	O
each	O	O

first	O	O
estimates	O	O
a	O	O
multiple	O	O
sequence	O	O

and	O	O
then	O	O
a	O	O

tree	O	B-Data_Structure

(	O	O

alignment	O	O

performs	O	O

iterations	O	O
,	O	O
but	O	O
a	O	O
host	O	O
of	O	O
options	O	O
enable	O	O

that	O	O
behavior	O	O
.	O	O

In	O	O
each	O	O
iteration	O	O

a	O	O

strategy	O	O
is	O	O

.	O	O

into	O	O
smaller	O	O

,	O	O

of	O	O
which	O	O
is	O	O
aligned	O	O
using	O	O
an	O	O
external	O	O
alignment	O	O
tool	O	O
(	O	O
the	O	O
default	O	O
is	O	O
MAFFT-L-ins-i	O	B-Application
)	O	O
.	O	O

These	O	O
subset	O	O

are	O	O
then	O	O
pairwise	O	O

(	O	O
by	O	O
default	O	O
using	O	O
Opal	O	B-Application
)	O	O
and	O	O
finally	O	O

pairwise	O	O
merged	O	O
alignments	O	O
are	O	O
merged	O	O
into	O	O
a	O	O
final	O	O
alignment	O	O
using	O	O
transitivity	O	O
merge	O	O
.	O	O

The	O	O
division	O	O
of	O	O
the	O	O
dataset	O	O
into	O	O
smaller	O	O
subsets	O	O
and	O	O
selecting	O	O
which	O	O
alignments	O	O
should	O	O
be	O	O
pairwise	O	O
merged	O	O
is	O	O

Flexgrid	O	B-Application
-	O	O
a	O	O
simple	O	O
grid	O	O
based	O	O
on	O	O
flexbox	O	B-Library
layout	O	O

No	O	O
more	O	O
floats	O	B-Variable
!	O	O

Regular	O	O
grid	O	O
layout	O	O
is	O	O
based	O	O
on	O	O
both	O	O
block	O	O
and	O	O
inline	O	O
flow	O	O
directions	O	O
,	O	O
however	O	O
,	O	O
the	O	O
flexbox	O	B-Library
(	O	O
or	O	O
just	O	O
flex	O	B-Library
)	O	O
layout	O	O
is	O	O
based	O	O
on	O	O
"	O	O
flex-flow	O	O
directions	O	O
"	O	O
.	O	O

Thus	O	O
float	B-Code_Block	B-Variable
and	O	O
clear	B-Code_Block	B-Variable
have	O	O
no	O	O
effect	O	O
.	O	O

Using	O	O
float	B-Code_Block	B-Variable
causes	O	O
the	O	O
display-property	B-Code_Block	B-Variable
to	O	O
compute	O	O
to	O	O
block	B-Code_Block	B-Variable
.	O	O

Using	O	O
flexbox	B-Code_Block	B-Library
also	O	O
means	O	O
less	O	O
JavaScript	O	B-Version
!	O	O

Everything	O	O
is	O	O
,	O	O
of	O	O
course	O	O
,	O	O
responsive	O	O
and	O	O
stacks	O	O
perfectly	O	O
.	O	O

Please	O	O
note	O	O
:	O	O
Flexbox	O	B-Library
is	O	O
only	O	O
partially	O	O
supported	O	O
by	O	O
IE10	O	B-Application
.	O	O

Any	O	O
IE-version	O	B-Application
lower	O	O
than	O	O
10	O	B-Version
does	O	O
not	O	O
support	O	O
flexbox	O	O
.	O	O

However	O	O
,	O	O
Flexgrid	O	B-Application
has	O	O
many	O	O
fallbacks	O	O
included	O	O
,	O	O
so	O	O
IE11	O	B-Application
should	O	O
be	O	O
safe	O	O
.	O	O

More	O	O
info	O	O
here	O	O
.	O	O

Flexgrid	O	B-Library
is	O	O
an	O	O
integral	O	O
part	O	O
of	O	O
the	O	O
upcoming	O	O
Nano	O	B-Library
Framework	O	I-Library
,	O	O
where	O	O
Flexgrid	O	B-Library
is	O	O
the	O	O
standard	O	O

.	O	O

Creating	O	O
a	O	O
count	O	O

-s	B-Code_Block	B-Code_Block
option	O	O

smaller	O	O
.	O	O

The	O	O
-q	B-Code_Block	B-Code_Block
